### System — 2026-07-01T18:59:50.072387

[Compressed Memory Summary]
The following is a compressed summary of earlier conversation turns, replacing the raw transcript to stay within the context window.

**Task:** Perform a full operational health check of the OWL swarm stack.

**Required actions:**
1. Call `blofin_get_stack_health` (no parameters) to obtain operational health snapshot (caches, feeds, errors, equity).
2. Call `blofin_get_swarm_learning_report` (no parameters) to retrieve the latest swarm learning report (what was learned, improved, fixed, with proof).
3. Combine the two responses into a strict JSON object with the following top‑level keys:
   - `status` (overall health status)
   - `issues` (list of identified problems)
   - `repair_actions` (recommended fixes)
   - `confidence` (numeric or textual confidence level)
   - `narrative` (human‑readable summary)

**Constraints:** Output must be valid JSON matching the schema above; no extra text.

**Available tools (relevant):**
- `blofin_get_stack_health` – returns health data.
- `blofin_get_swarm_learning_report` – returns learning report.

### Key Insights & Issues
1. **Rate‑limit (429) on account balance** – live equity data could not be fetched; the system used a cached snapshot. This is expected under heavy API load but should trigger a back‑off and use cached equity for the remainder of the cycle.
2. **All open positions lack TP/SL** – immediate action required to protect downside and lock‑in upside. Follow the rule to place TP/SL for `STABLE‑USDT`, `BAS‑USDT`, and `ADA‑USDT`.
3. **Blocked symbols** prevent any new orders on the current positions. The pipeline must either:
   - Wait for the block to clear next cycle, **or**
   - Scan the remaining universe (511‑2 = 509 symbols) for a new candidate that is not blocked.
4. **Portfolio health**: Net unrealized P&L is positive (+≈ $0.180 USDT) despite a tiny loss on ADA. Overall equity is modest ($2.33) with $1.69 available for new margin.
5. **No critical errors** besides the rate‑limit warning; stack health is **healthy** but monitoring should watch for repeated 429s.

### Immediate Recommended Actions
- **Place TP/SL** for the three open positions using `blofin_place_tpsl` (or `blofin_ensure_position_tpsl`).  
- **Respect blocks**: do not issue new buy for ADA‑USDT or new sell for STABLE‑USDT / BAS‑USDT this cycle.  
- **If a trade is needed**, run a universe scan to select an alternative symbol not in the blocked lists.  
- **Handle 429**: back‑off API calls, rely on cached equity for the rest of the cycle, and schedule a retry after ~120 s.  

**Overall status:** Stack is **healthy** with minor warnings; the primary focus is adding TP/SL and managing the rate‑limit fallback.
